# KAIA Call Tables - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/kaia/decoded/call-tables#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Decoded

KAIA Call Tables

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/kaia/decoded/call-tables#overview)
    
*   [Decoding](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/kaia/decoded/call-tables#decoding)
    
*   [Multiple Instances](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/kaia/decoded/call-tables#multiple-instances)
    
*   [Common misconceptions](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/kaia/decoded/call-tables#common-misconceptions)
    
*   [Further Reading](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/kaia/decoded/call-tables#further-reading)
    

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/kaia/decoded/call-tables#overview)

Overview
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On Dune, we parse all message calls and transactions made to smart contracts in their own tables. This allows us to isolate the logic of a specific smart contract and analyze how it interacts with other smart contracts. The data is stored in the format: `[projectname_blockchain].[contractName]_call_[functionName]` This allows us to analyze how a specific function is used in a smart contract, and how often it is called, as well as how it interacts with other smart contracts. Call tables always originate from the `traces` table, which contains all the transactions and message calls on the Ethereum network. We parse the `data` field of the `traces` table to decode the function call and parameters.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/kaia/decoded/call-tables#decoding)

Decoding
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a transaction is sent to a smart contract on the Ethereum network, it contains a `data` field. This `data` field is the encoded function call and parameters. Dune decodes this data and stores it in the corresponding table. For example, when a transaction is sent to the [Uniswap v3 factory](https://etherscan.io/address/0x1f98431c8ad98523631ae4a59f267346ea31f984#code)
 contract on the Ethereum network, Dune will decode the `data` field and store it in the table: `uniswap_v3_ethereum.Factory_call_createPool`

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/kaia/decoded/call-tables#multiple-instances)

Multiple Instances
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For a contract where multiple instances exist, we will decode all calls to all instances of this smart contract into one table. If there are transactions calling the `swap` function of any instance of the [Uniswap v3 pair](https://etherscan.io/address/0x8f8ef111b67c04eb1641f5ff19ee54cda062f163#writeContract)
 contract, we will decode this data into the table `uniswap_v3_ethereum.Pair_call_swap`. The `pair` contract is a template contract and there are many instances of it, each with its own address. The column `contract_address` will indicate the address of the instance of the pair contract that was called.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/kaia/decoded/call-tables#common-misconceptions)

Common misconceptions
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

One thing to keep in mind here is that [web3.js](https://web3js.readthedocs.io/)
, [web3.py](https://web3py.readthedocs.io/en/stable)
 and all other methods of (locally) calling a `pure`, `read`, or `constant` function do not broadcast or publish anything on the blockchain and are therefore not recorded in Dune. However, if one of these functions is invoked by another smart contract in the context of a transaction, this will be broadcast on the chain and therefore accessible in Dune. In short: **State data stored in the memory of a smart contract is not available on Dune!** A good example of this is the function `decimals` of the [erc20 token contract](https://etherscan.io/token/0x1f9840a85d5af5bf1d1762f925bdaddc4201f984#readContract)
 `Uni` which is a `constant` state variable that is able to be accessed through an automatically created “[getter function](https://docs.soliditylang.org/en/v0.7.4/contracts.html#getter-functions)
”. Should a smart contract invoke this function in the context of transaction, this message call will be recorded in the Dune table [`uniswap."UNI_call_decimals"`](https://dune.com/queries/741354)
. This is in contrast to anyone calling this function locally using web3.py/web3.js or using the Etherscan frontend to access this state. These local calls are not recorded in Dune.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/kaia/decoded/call-tables#further-reading)

Further Reading
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[What is the difference between a transaction and a call?\
--------------------------------------------------------](https://ethereum.stackexchange.com/questions/765/what-is-the-difference-between-a-transaction-and-a-call)
[Soliditylang.org documentation\
------------------------------](https://docs.soliditylang.org/en/v0.8.13/contracts.html#function-visibility)
[How Calldata is Encoded\
-----------------------](https://degatchi.com/articles/reading-raw-evm-calldata)

# kaia.logs_decoded - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/kaia/decoded/logs-decoded#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Navigation

Decoded

kaia.logs\_decoded

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `logs_decoded` table contains decoded logs from kaia transactions. The table matches `topic0` to the event signature and the corresponding event name. The table does not contain the full event data and is not suitable for analysis of smart contract level data. For that, use the specific event tables as described in [Event Logs](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/kaia/decoded/event-logs)
.This table is great for gaining a high level understanding of the types of events that are being emitted by a smart contract or smart contracts of a certain protocol.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

# dex.trades on lens - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/curated-data/dex/dex-trades#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

DEX

dex.trades on lens

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

This is a cross-chain table but can be filtered for lens transactions.

Table Description
-----------------

The `dex.trades` table captures detailed data on trades executed via decentralized exchanges (DEXs). This table captures all raw trade events that happen across all liqudity pools. It provides a comprehensive view of the entire trade execution process, detailing the specific paths and liquidity sources utilized.

Functional Overview
-------------------

The `dex.trades` table provides an in-depth view of trades on decentralized exchanges like Uniswap or Curve. This table includes entries for each segment of a trade that passes through different liquidity pools, as well as single-step trades. For example, a user may initiate a trade to swap USDC for PEPE. If this trade is executed through multiple liquidity pools, such as USDC-WETH and WETH-PEPE, the `dex.trades` table will record each segment of the trade as a separate entry. Conversely, a single-step trade, such as directly swapping USDC for ETH, will be recorded as a single entry.This detailed approach allows for granular analysis of trade execution paths, enabling users to:

*   **Analyze Liquidity Sources:** Understand which liquidity pools are used and how they interact in both single-step and multi-step trades.
*   **Track Trade Execution Paths:** Follow the exact route a trade takes across different DEXs and liquidity pools
*   **Assess Slippage and Execution Quality:** Evaluate the impact of each step on the overall trade execution, including slippage and price changes.
*   **Monitor Market Dynamics:** Gain insights into the behavior and dynamics of different liquidity pools and DEXs over time.

Table Coverage
--------------

The following table shows which projects and versions of those projects are covered in the `dex.trades` table on lens.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

# katana.traces - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/katana/raw/traces#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Raw

katana.traces

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `katana.traces` table contains the traces of the transactions executed on the Ethereum Virtual Machine (EVM). It includes the traces of the transaction and the traces of the internal transactions. Traces are the result of the execution of the transaction and are used to debug and understand the execution of the transaction. They are also known as \`internal transactions\` and can be used to understand the execution of a transaction.

This is the raw version of this table. If the chain is a Fully Managed chain, decoded transaction calls will be available, see [call tables](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/katana/decoded/call-tables)
 section. If this is a Hosted chain, decoded call tables will not be available.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Example
-------

### Querying traces for a specific transaction hash

    SELECT *
    FROM katana.traces
    WHERE tx_hash = 0xb30d6d67cf7d148c2257bf598c5f5cdf5912a3d05c7d3b000398d675d2fa912c

NFT.trades on lens

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)

[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

This is a cross-chain table but can be filtered for lens transactions.

Table Description
-----------------

The \`nft.trades\` table on Dune Analytics is central to capturing and analyzing Non-Fungible Token (NFT) transactions across various marketplaces. It is a pivotal resource for dissecting the intricacies of NFT trade execution, market behavior, and collector activity within the NFT space.

Usage
-----

The \`nft.trades\` table serves as an essential tool for delving into the NFT market's complexities. It offers a detailed snapshot of each NFT transaction, encompassing data points such as sale price, transaction timestamp, buyer and seller addresses, and the specific NFT assets involved. This table allows analysts to explore trends in NFT valuation, trading volumes, and marketplace dynamics, providing insights into the evolving landscape of digital collectibles and art.

# katana.transactions - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/katana/raw/transactions#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Raw

katana.transactions

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `katana.transactions` table contains information about all transactions on the katana blockchain. Each row represents a single transaction and includes information such as block number, hash, timestamp, sender, recipient, value, gas, gas price, and more. Transactions are the fundamental unit of interaction with the katana blockchain. Transactions are created by users and are used to send value, deploy smart contracts, and interact with smart contracts.

This is the raw version of this table. If the chain is a Fully Managed chain, decoded transaction calls will be available, see [call tables](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/katana/decoded/call-tables)
 section. If this is a Hosted chain, decoded call tables will not be available.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Examples
--------

### Show all transactions sent by a specific address

    SELECT * 
    FROM katana.transactions WHERE "from" = '0x50A1b5c358F8D34F0d35aA2f10742c46054E247e'
    

### Count the number of transactions per block

    SELECT 
        block_number, 
        COUNT(*)
    FROM katana.transactions
    GROUP BY 1
    ORDER BY 1 DESC
    LIMIT 10
    

### Show the top 10 transactions with the highest gas price

    SELECT 
        hash, 
        gas_price
    FROM katana.transactions
    ORDER BY gas_price DESC
    LIMIT 10

# Lens Call Tables - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Decoded

Lens Call Tables

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables#overview)
    
*   [Decoding](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables#decoding)
    
*   [Multiple Instances](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables#multiple-instances)
    
*   [Common misconceptions](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables#common-misconceptions)
    
*   [Further Reading](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables#further-reading)
    

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables#overview)

Overview
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On Dune, we parse all message calls and transactions made to smart contracts in their own tables. This allows us to isolate the logic of a specific smart contract and analyze how it interacts with other smart contracts. The data is stored in the format: `[projectname_blockchain].[contractName]_call_[functionName]` This allows us to analyze how a specific function is used in a smart contract, and how often it is called, as well as how it interacts with other smart contracts. Call tables always originate from the `traces` table, which contains all the transactions and message calls on the Ethereum network. We parse the `data` field of the `traces` table to decode the function call and parameters.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables#decoding)

Decoding
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a transaction is sent to a smart contract on the Ethereum network, it contains a `data` field. This `data` field is the encoded function call and parameters. Dune decodes this data and stores it in the corresponding table. For example, when a transaction is sent to the [Uniswap v3 factory](https://etherscan.io/address/0x1f98431c8ad98523631ae4a59f267346ea31f984#code)
 contract on the Ethereum network, Dune will decode the `data` field and store it in the table: `uniswap_v3_ethereum.Factory_call_createPool`

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables#multiple-instances)

Multiple Instances
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For a contract where multiple instances exist, we will decode all calls to all instances of this smart contract into one table. If there are transactions calling the `swap` function of any instance of the [Uniswap v3 pair](https://etherscan.io/address/0x8f8ef111b67c04eb1641f5ff19ee54cda062f163#writeContract)
 contract, we will decode this data into the table `uniswap_v3_ethereum.Pair_call_swap`. The `pair` contract is a template contract and there are many instances of it, each with its own address. The column `contract_address` will indicate the address of the instance of the pair contract that was called.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables#common-misconceptions)

Common misconceptions
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

One thing to keep in mind here is that [web3.js](https://web3js.readthedocs.io/)
, [web3.py](https://web3py.readthedocs.io/en/stable)
 and all other methods of (locally) calling a `pure`, `read`, or `constant` function do not broadcast or publish anything on the blockchain and are therefore not recorded in Dune. However, if one of these functions is invoked by another smart contract in the context of a transaction, this will be broadcast on the chain and therefore accessible in Dune. In short: **State data stored in the memory of a smart contract is not available on Dune!** A good example of this is the function `decimals` of the [erc20 token contract](https://etherscan.io/token/0x1f9840a85d5af5bf1d1762f925bdaddc4201f984#readContract)
 `Uni` which is a `constant` state variable that is able to be accessed through an automatically created “[getter function](https://docs.soliditylang.org/en/v0.7.4/contracts.html#getter-functions)
”. Should a smart contract invoke this function in the context of transaction, this message call will be recorded in the Dune table [`uniswap."UNI_call_decimals"`](https://dune.com/queries/741354)
. This is in contrast to anyone calling this function locally using web3.py/web3.js or using the Etherscan frontend to access this state. These local calls are not recorded in Dune.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables#further-reading)

Further Reading
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[What is the difference between a transaction and a call?\
--------------------------------------------------------](https://ethereum.stackexchange.com/questions/765/what-is-the-difference-between-a-transaction-and-a-call)
[Soliditylang.org documentation\
------------------------------](https://docs.soliditylang.org/en/v0.8.13/contracts.html#function-visibility)
[How Calldata is Encoded\
-----------------------](https://degatchi.com/articles/reading-raw-evm-calldata)

For that, use the specific event tables as described in [Event Logs](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/event-logs)

# lens.traces_decoded - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/traces-decoded#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Navigation

Decoded

lens.traces\_decoded

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `traces_decoded` table contains decoded traces from lens transactions. The table matches `MethodID`, which consists of the first 4 bytes of any eth call, to the trace signature and the corresponding Method name. The table does not contain the full trace data and is not suitable for analysis of smart contract level data. For that, use the specific event tables as described in [Call-tables](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/traces-decoded)
.This table is great for gaining a high level understanding of the types of events that are being emitted by a smart contract or smart contracts of a certain protocol.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

# lens.blocks - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/raw/blocks#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Raw

lens.blocks

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table description
-----------------

The `lens.blocks` table contains information about blocks in the lens blockchain. A block is a collection of transactions that are hashed and added to the blockchain. Each block contains a reference to the previous block, known as the parent hash, and a timestamp. The table contains information about each block, such as the block number, the block hash, the block size, the number of transactions, and the gas used.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Examples
--------

### Show the most recent blocks

    SELECT
        number,
        hash, 
        size,
        gas_used
      FROM lens.blocks
      ORDER BY number DESC
      LIMIT 10

### Show the number of blocks mined each day

    SELECT
        date_trunc('day', time) AS day,
        count(distinct number)
      FROM lens.blocks
      GROUP BY day
      ORDER BY day DESC

### Show the number of transactions in each block

    SELECT
        number,
        count(*)
      FROM lens.blocks
      GROUP BY 1 
      LIMIT 10

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

# lens.creation_traces - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/raw/creation-traces#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Raw

lens.creation\_traces

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `lens.creation_traces` table contains information about the creation of smart contracts on the lens blockchain. This includes the address of the contract, the address of the creator, the block number at which the contract was created, the transaction hash, and the contract's bytecode. This table is useful for understanding the deployment of smart contracts on the lens blockchain.

This table is a subset of the `traces` table, which contains information about all traces on the lens blockchain. The `creation_traces` table is filtered to only include traces that create new smart contracts. The filter for this is `type = 'create'` .

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Examples
--------

### Show the creation of a specific smart contract

    SELECT * FROM lens.creation_traces
    WHERE contract_address = 0x06012c8cf97bead5deae237070f9587f8e7a266d

### Show the creation of smart contracts by a specific creator

    SELECT * FROM lens.creation_traces
    WHERE "from" = 0x0d4a11d5eeaac28ec3f61d100da81f6a1b65c9d6

### Show the creation of smart contracts in the last 10 days

    SELECT 
        date_trunc('day', block_time) AS day,
        COUNT(*)
    FROM lens.creation_traces
    GROUP BY 1
    ORDER BY 1 DESC
    LIMIT 10

YesNo

# lens.logs - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/raw/logs#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Raw

lens.logs

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `lens.logs` table represents the logs generated by the Ethereum Virtual Machine (EVM) when a contract is executed. Logs are a way to store data on the blockchain. Logs originate from events that occur during the execution of a smart contract. A log consists of:

*   topic list: a list of 0 to 3 32-byte data topics. `Topic0` is the hash of the signature of the event (indexed), and the remaining topics are indexed parameters of the event.
*   data: contains non-indexed data.

This is the raw version of this table. If the chain is a Fully Managed chain, decoded transaction calls will be available, see [call tables](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables)
 section. If this is a Hosted chain, decoded call tables will not be available.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Examples
--------

### Filter the logs for a specific contract

    SELECT *
    FROM lens.logs
    WHERE contract_address = 0x06012c8cf97bead5deae237070f9587f8e7a266d
    LIMIT 10

### Filter the logs for a specific topic

    SELECT *
    FROM lens.logs
    WHERE topic0 = 0xddf252ad1be2c89b69c2b068fc378daa952ba7f163c4a11628f55a4df523b3ef
    

### Show the logs of a specific block

    SELECT *
    FROM lens.logs
    WHERE evt_block_number = 1000000
    

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Raise issue](https://github.com/duneanalytics/dune-docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/data-catalog/evm/lens/raw/logs)

# dex_aggregator.trades on linea - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/linea/curated-data/dex/dex-aggregator-trades#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

DEX

dex\_aggregator.trades on linea

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

This table is a cross-chain table but can be filtered for linea transactions.

Table Description
-----------------

The `dex_aggregator.trades` table captures high-level data on trades executed via decentralized exchange (DEX) aggregators. These aggregators aggregate liquidity from multiple DEXs to provide users with the best possible trade execution. Unlike the `dex.trades` table, which records each intermediary step of a trade, `dex_aggregator.trades` condenses the trade data to reflect the user's intended trade, presenting it as a single entry.

Functional Overview
-------------------

Users can expect the `dex_aggregator.trades` table to provide a high-level view of DEX trades facilitated by aggregators. This table simplifies trade records by showing a single entry for trades that may involve multiple DEXs and liquidity pools. For instance, a user might initiate a trade to swap USDC for PEPE via a DEX aggregator. The aggregator might route this trade through several liquidity pools such as WETH-USDC and WETH-PEPE, but `dex_aggregator.trades` will record it as a single USDC → PEPE trade.Complimentary to `dex_aggregator.trades` is the `dex.trades` table, where detailed trade executions are recorded. This table captures the granular steps of each trade, including interactions with different liquidity pools. The volume routed through aggregators is also recorded in the `dex.trades` table. One row in `dex_aggregator.trades` corresponds to one or more rows in `dex.trades`, providing a comprehensive view of the detailed execution path that aggregated trades take.

Coverage
--------

The following table shows which projects and versions of those projects are covered in the `dex.trades` table on linea.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Raise issue](https://github.com/duneanalytics/dune-docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/data-catalog/evm/linea/curated-data/dex/dex-aggregator-trades)

# NFT.trades on linea - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/linea/curated-data/nft/nft-trades#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

NFT

NFT.trades on linea

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

This is a cross-chain table but can be filtered for linea transactions.

Table Description
-----------------

The \`nft.trades\` table on Dune Analytics is central to capturing and analyzing Non-Fungible Token (NFT) transactions across various marketplaces. It is a pivotal resource for dissecting the intricacies of NFT trade execution, market behavior, and collector activity within the NFT space.

Usage
-----

The \`nft.trades\` table serves as an essential tool for delving into the NFT market's complexities. It offers a detailed snapshot of each NFT transaction, encompassing data points such as sale price, transaction timestamp, buyer and seller addresses, and the specific NFT assets involved. This table allows analysts to explore trends in NFT valuation, trading volumes, and marketplace dynamics, providing insights into the evolving landscape of digital collectibles and art.

Table Coverage
--------------

The following table shows which projects and versions of those projects are covered in the `dex.trades` table on linea.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

# dex.trades on mantle - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/curated-data/dex/dex-trades#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

DEX

dex.trades on mantle

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

This is a cross-chain table but can be filtered for mantle transactions.

Table Description
-----------------

The `dex.trades` table captures detailed data on trades executed via decentralized exchanges (DEXs). This table captures all raw trade events that happen across all liqudity pools. It provides a comprehensive view of the entire trade execution process, detailing the specific paths and liquidity sources utilized.

Functional Overview
-------------------

The `dex.trades` table provides an in-depth view of trades on decentralized exchanges like Uniswap or Curve. This table includes entries for each segment of a trade that passes through different liquidity pools, as well as single-step trades. For example, a user may initiate a trade to swap USDC for PEPE. If this trade is executed through multiple liquidity pools, such as USDC-WETH and WETH-PEPE, the `dex.trades` table will record each segment of the trade as a separate entry. Conversely, a single-step trade, such as directly swapping USDC for ETH, will be recorded as a single entry.This detailed approach allows for granular analysis of trade execution paths, enabling users to:

*   **Analyze Liquidity Sources:** Understand which liquidity pools are used and how they interact in both single-step and multi-step trades.
*   **Track Trade Execution Paths:** Follow the exact route a trade takes across different DEXs and liquidity pools
*   **Assess Slippage and Execution Quality:** Evaluate the impact of each step on the overall trade execution, including slippage and price changes.
*   **Monitor Market Dynamics:** Gain insights into the behavior and dynamics of different liquidity pools and DEXs over time.

Table Coverage
--------------

The following table shows which projects and versions of those projects are covered in the `dex.trades` table on mantle.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

DEX

dex.trades on linea

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

This is a cross-chain table but can be filtered for linea transactions.

Table Description
-----------------

The `dex.trades` table captures detailed data on trades executed via decentralized exchanges (DEXs). This table captures all raw trade events that happen across all liqudity pools. It provides a comprehensive view of the entire trade execution process, detailing the specific paths and liquidity sources utilized.

Functional Overview
-------------------

The `dex.trades` table provides an in-depth view of trades on decentralized exchanges like Uniswap or Curve. This table includes entries for each segment of a trade that passes through different liquidity pools, as well as single-step trades. For example, a user may initiate a trade to swap USDC for PEPE. If this trade is executed through multiple liquidity pools, such as USDC-WETH and WETH-PEPE, the `dex.trades` table will record each segment of the trade as a separate entry. Conversely, a single-step trade, such as directly swapping USDC for ETH, will be recorded as a single entry.This detailed approach allows for granular analysis of trade execution paths, enabling users to:

*   **Analyze Liquidity Sources:** Understand which liquidity pools are used and how they interact in both single-step and multi-step trades.
*   **Track Trade Execution Paths:** Follow the exact route a trade takes across different DEXs and liquidity pools
*   **Assess Slippage and Execution Quality:** Evaluate the impact of each step on the overall trade execution, including slippage and price changes.
*   **Monitor Market Dynamics:** Gain insights into the behavior and dynamics of different liquidity pools and DEXs over time.

Table Coverage
--------------

The following table shows which projects and versions of those projects are covered in the `dex.trades` table on linea.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

On this page

*   [Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/linea/overview#data-catalog)
    

Linea is an EVM-equivalent network, scaling the Ethereum experience. Secured with a zero-knowledge rollup to Ethereum, built on lattice-based cryptography, and powered by Consensys. Linea behaves like Ethereum, but with a higher throughput and lower fees.

[Linea docs\

# Mantle Overview - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/overview#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Mantle

Mantle Overview

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

On this page

*   [Key Features](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/overview#key-features)
    
*   [Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/overview#data-catalog)
    

Mantle Network is dedicated to building an EVM-compatible scaling solution for Ethereum. This means that all contracts and tools running on Ethereum can operate on the Mantle Network with minimal modifications. Taking advantage of its modular architecture, Mantle Network combines an optimistic rollup with various innovative data availability solutions, providing cheaper and more accessible data availability while inheriting the security of Ethereum. Mantle’s design philosophy aims to offer users a less costly and more user-friendly experience, provide developers with a simpler and more flexible development environment, and deliver a comprehensive set of infrastructure for the next wave of mass-adopted dApps. As an Ethereum L2, Mantle Network offers the security, stability, and scalability necessary to support your onchain applications. Developers can deploy any EVM-compatible codebase and smoothly transition users and assets from Ethereum L1 and other compatible chains.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/overview#key-features)

Key Features
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Built as a Rollup**: Utilizes Ethereum validators and consensus protocols to significantly reduce gas fees, decrease latency, and increase throughput. Users can customize transaction confirmation requirements to provide near real-time confirmation latency with minimal security settings.
*   **Modular Architecture**: Unlike traditional monolithic chains that execute transaction execution, consensus, settlement, and storage at the same network layer, Mantle separates these functions into individual modules as a modular chain. These include an EVM-compatible execution layer developed by Mantle for transaction execution, a consensus layer and settlement layer completed on Ethereum, and an external DA component (currently Mantle DA powered by EigenDA technology; we will switch to EigenDA upon its mainnet stable launch).
*   **Secured by Ethereum**: L2 state transitions are verified by Ethereum validators, undergoing the same consensus and settlement processes as L1 transactions.
*   **Modular Data Availability**: Independent DA modules, such as Mantle DA powered by EigenLayer’s EigenDA technology. According to internal assessments, this translates to potential cost savings of more than 90% compared to on-chain L1.

[Mantle documentation\
--------------------\
\
Explore comprehensive documentation on Mantle, detailing its architecture, protocol, and resources for developers.](https://mantle.network/docs)

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/overview#data-catalog)

Data Catalog
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Logs\
----\
\
Detailed event logs from smart contracts, providing insights into interactions within the Mantle network.](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/raw/logs)
[Blocks\
------\
\
Information on blocks, illustrating the operational capacity and activity levels on Mantle.](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/raw/blocks)
[Transactions\
------------\
\
Extensive transaction data, showcasing the efficiency and execution of operations on Mantle.](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/raw/transactions)
[Decoded\
-------\
\
Enhanced transaction data decoded for better analysis and understanding of contract executions.](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/overview)

# mantle.blocks - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/raw/blocks#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Raw

mantle.blocks

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table description
-----------------

The `mantle.blocks` table contains information about blocks in the mantle blockchain. A block is a collection of transactions that are hashed and added to the blockchain. Each block contains a reference to the previous block, known as the parent hash, and a timestamp. The table contains information about each block, such as the block number, the block hash, the block size, the number of transactions, and the gas used.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Examples
--------

### Show the most recent blocks

    SELECT
        number,
        hash, 
        size,
        gas_used
      FROM mantle.blocks
      ORDER BY number DESC
      LIMIT 10

### Show the number of blocks mined each day

    SELECT
        date_trunc('day', time) AS day,
        count(distinct number)
      FROM mantle.blocks
      GROUP BY day
      ORDER BY day DESC

### Show the number of transactions in each block

    SELECT
        number,
        count(*)
      FROM mantle.blocks
      GROUP BY 1 
      LIMIT 10

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

# mantle.creation_traces - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/raw/creation-traces#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Raw

mantle.creation\_traces

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `mantle.creation_traces` table contains information about the creation of smart contracts on the mantle blockchain. This includes the address of the contract, the address of the creator, the block number at which the contract was created, the transaction hash, and the contract's bytecode. This table is useful for understanding the deployment of smart contracts on the mantle blockchain.

This table is a subset of the `traces` table, which contains information about all traces on the mantle blockchain. The `creation_traces` table is filtered to only include traces that create new smart contracts. The filter for this is `type = 'create'` .

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Examples
--------

### Show the creation of a specific smart contract

    SELECT * FROM mantle.creation_traces
    WHERE contract_address = 0x06012c8cf97bead5deae237070f9587f8e7a266d

### Show the creation of smart contracts by a specific creator

    SELECT * FROM mantle.creation_traces
    WHERE "from" = 0x0d4a11d5eeaac28ec3f61d100da81f6a1b65c9d6

### Show the creation of smart contracts in the last 10 days

    SELECT 
        date_trunc('day', block_time) AS day,
        COUNT(*)
    FROM mantle.creation_traces
    GROUP BY 1
    ORDER BY 1 DESC
    LIMIT 10

# lens.traces - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/raw/traces#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Raw

lens.traces

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

You may see duplicate records in the `traces` table for the Lens chain. This is not a bug, but a result of trace calls appearing twice within the same transaction. These consecutive calls—an outer and an inner call—are identical except for their gas values. They share the same `from`, `to`, `input`, `output`, `success`, and `value` fields.

Table Description
-----------------

The `lens.traces` table contains the traces of the transactions executed on the Ethereum Virtual Machine (EVM). It includes the traces of the transaction and the traces of the internal transactions. Traces are the result of the execution of the transaction and are used to debug and understand the execution of the transaction. They are also known as \`internal transactions\` and can be used to understand the execution of a transaction.

This is the raw version of this table. If the chain is a Fully Managed chain, decoded transaction calls will be available, see [call tables](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables)
 section. If this is a Hosted chain, decoded call tables will not be available.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Example
-------

### Querying traces for a specific transaction hash

    SELECT *
    FROM lens.traces
    WHERE tx_hash = 0xb30d6d67cf7d148c2257bf598c5f5cdf5912a3d05c7d3b000398d675d2fa912c
    

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Raise issue](https://github.com/duneanalytics/dune-docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/data-catalog/evm/lens/raw/traces)

[Transactions](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/raw/transactions)
[Lens Decoded Overview](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/overview)

⌘I

# lens.transactions - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/raw/transactions#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Raw

lens.transactions

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `lens.transactions` table contains information about all transactions on the lens blockchain. Each row represents a single transaction and includes information such as block number, hash, timestamp, sender, recipient, value, gas, gas price, and more. Transactions are the fundamental unit of interaction with the lens blockchain. Transactions are created by users and are used to send value, deploy smart contracts, and interact with smart contracts.

This is the raw version of this table. If the chain is a Fully Managed chain, decoded transaction calls will be available, see [call tables](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/lens/decoded/call-tables)
 section. If this is a Hosted chain, decoded call tables will not be available.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Examples
--------

### Show all transactions sent by a specific address

    SELECT * 
    FROM lens.transactions WHERE "from" = '0x50A1b5c358F8D34F0d35aA2f10742c46054E247e'
    

### Count the number of transactions per block

    SELECT 
        block_number, 
        COUNT(*)
    FROM lens.transactions
    GROUP BY 1
    ORDER BY 1 DESC
    LIMIT 10
    

### Show the top 10 transactions with the highest gas price

    SELECT 
        hash, 
        gas_price
    FROM lens.transactions
    ORDER BY gas_price DESC
    LIMIT 10

Decoded

linea.traces\_decoded

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `traces_decoded` table contains decoded traces from linea transactions. The table matches `MethodID`, which consists of the first 4 bytes of any eth call, to the trace signature and the corresponding Method name. The table does not contain the full trace data and is not suitable for analysis of smart contract level data. For that, use the specific event tables as described in [Call-tables](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/linea/decoded/traces-decoded)
.This table is great for gaining a high level understanding of the types of events that are being emitted by a smart contract or smart contracts of a certain protocol.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

# linea.logs - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/linea/raw/logs#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Raw

linea.logs

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `linea.logs` table represents the logs generated by the Ethereum Virtual Machine (EVM) when a contract is executed. Logs are a way to store data on the blockchain. Logs originate from events that occur during the execution of a smart contract. A log consists of:

*   topic list: a list of 0 to 3 32-byte data topics. `Topic0` is the hash of the signature of the event (indexed), and the remaining topics are indexed parameters of the event.
*   data: contains non-indexed data.

This is the raw version of this table. If the chain is a Fully Managed chain, decoded transaction calls will be available, see [call tables](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/linea/decoded/call-tables)
 section. If this is a Hosted chain, decoded call tables will not be available.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Examples
--------

### Filter the logs for a specific contract

    SELECT *
    FROM linea.logs
    WHERE contract_address = 0x06012c8cf97bead5deae237070f9587f8e7a266d
    LIMIT 10

### Filter the logs for a specific topic

    SELECT *
    FROM linea.logs
    WHERE topic0 = 0xddf252ad1be2c89b69c2b068fc378daa952ba7f163c4a11628f55a4df523b3ef
    

### Show the logs of a specific block

    SELECT *
    FROM linea.logs
    WHERE evt_block_number = 1000000

YesNo

# mantle.transactions - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/raw/transactions#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Navigation

Raw

mantle.transactions

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `mantle.transactions` table contains information about all transactions on the mantle blockchain. Each row represents a single transaction and includes information such as block number, hash, timestamp, sender, recipient, value, gas, gas price, and more. Transactions are the fundamental unit of interaction with the mantle blockchain. Transactions are created by users and are used to send value, deploy smart contracts, and interact with smart contracts.

This is the raw version of this table. If the chain is a Fully Managed chain, decoded transaction calls will be available, see [call tables](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables)
 section. If this is a Hosted chain, decoded call tables will not be available.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Examples
--------

### Show all transactions sent by a specific address

    SELECT * 
    FROM mantle.transactions WHERE "from" = '0x50A1b5c358F8D34F0d35aA2f10742c46054E247e'
    

### Count the number of transactions per block

    SELECT 
        block_number, 
        COUNT(*)
    FROM mantle.transactions
    GROUP BY 1
    ORDER BY 1 DESC
    LIMIT 10
    

### Show the top 10 transactions with the highest gas price

    SELECT 
        hash, 
        gas_price
    FROM mantle.transactions
    ORDER BY gas_price DESC
    LIMIT 10

# mantle.logs - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/raw/logs#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Raw

mantle.logs

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `mantle.logs` table represents the logs generated by the Ethereum Virtual Machine (EVM) when a contract is executed. Logs are a way to store data on the blockchain. Logs originate from events that occur during the execution of a smart contract. A log consists of:

*   topic list: a list of 0 to 3 32-byte data topics. `Topic0` is the hash of the signature of the event (indexed), and the remaining topics are indexed parameters of the event.
*   data: contains non-indexed data.

This is the raw version of this table. If the chain is a Fully Managed chain, decoded transaction calls will be available, see [call tables](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables)
 section. If this is a Hosted chain, decoded call tables will not be available.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Examples
--------

### Filter the logs for a specific contract

    SELECT *
    FROM mantle.logs
    WHERE contract_address = 0x06012c8cf97bead5deae237070f9587f8e7a266d
    LIMIT 10

### Filter the logs for a specific topic

    SELECT *
    FROM mantle.logs
    WHERE topic0 = 0xddf252ad1be2c89b69c2b068fc378daa952ba7f163c4a11628f55a4df523b3ef
    

### Show the logs of a specific block

    SELECT *
    FROM mantle.logs
    WHERE evt_block_number = 1000000

# Mantle Call Tables - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Decoded

Mantle Call Tables

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables#overview)
    
*   [Decoding](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables#decoding)
    
*   [Multiple Instances](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables#multiple-instances)
    
*   [Common misconceptions](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables#common-misconceptions)
    
*   [Further Reading](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables#further-reading)
    

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables#overview)

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On Dune, we parse all message calls and transactions made to smart contracts in their own tables. This allows us to isolate the logic of a specific smart contract and analyze how it interacts with other smart contracts. The data is stored in the format: `[projectname_blockchain].[contractName]_call_[functionName]` This allows us to analyze how a specific function is used in a smart contract, and how often it is called, as well as how it interacts with other smart contracts. Call tables always originate from the `traces` table, which contains all the transactions and message calls on the Ethereum network. We parse the `data` field of the `traces` table to decode the function call and parameters.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables#decoding)

Decoding
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a transaction is sent to a smart contract on the Ethereum network, it contains a `data` field. This `data` field is the encoded function call and parameters. Dune decodes this data and stores it in the corresponding table. For example, when a transaction is sent to the [Uniswap v3 factory](https://etherscan.io/address/0x1f98431c8ad98523631ae4a59f267346ea31f984#code)
 contract on the Ethereum network, Dune will decode the `data` field and store it in the table: `uniswap_v3_ethereum.Factory_call_createPool`

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables#multiple-instances)

Multiple Instances
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For a contract where multiple instances exist, we will decode all calls to all instances of this smart contract into one table. If there are transactions calling the `swap` function of any instance of the [Uniswap v3 pair](https://etherscan.io/address/0x8f8ef111b67c04eb1641f5ff19ee54cda062f163#writeContract)
 contract, we will decode this data into the table `uniswap_v3_ethereum.Pair_call_swap`. The `pair` contract is a template contract and there are many instances of it, each with its own address. The column `contract_address` will indicate the address of the instance of the pair contract that was called.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables#common-misconceptions)

Common misconceptions
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

One thing to keep in mind here is that [web3.js](https://web3js.readthedocs.io/)
, [web3.py](https://web3py.readthedocs.io/en/stable)
 and all other methods of (locally) calling a `pure`, `read`, or `constant` function do not broadcast or publish anything on the blockchain and are therefore not recorded in Dune. However, if one of these functions is invoked by another smart contract in the context of a transaction, this will be broadcast on the chain and therefore accessible in Dune. In short: **State data stored in the memory of a smart contract is not available on Dune!** A good example of this is the function `decimals` of the [erc20 token contract](https://etherscan.io/token/0x1f9840a85d5af5bf1d1762f925bdaddc4201f984#readContract)
 `Uni` which is a `constant` state variable that is able to be accessed through an automatically created “[getter function](https://docs.soliditylang.org/en/v0.7.4/contracts.html#getter-functions)
”. Should a smart contract invoke this function in the context of transaction, this message call will be recorded in the Dune table [`uniswap."UNI_call_decimals"`](https://dune.com/queries/741354)
. This is in contrast to anyone calling this function locally using web3.py/web3.js or using the Etherscan frontend to access this state. These local calls are not recorded in Dune.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables#further-reading)

Further Reading
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[What is the difference between a transaction and a call?\
--------------------------------------------------------](https://ethereum.stackexchange.com/questions/765/what-is-the-difference-between-a-transaction-and-a-call)
[Soliditylang.org documentation\
------------------------------](https://docs.soliditylang.org/en/v0.8.13/contracts.html#function-visibility)
[How Calldata is Encoded\
-----------------------](https://degatchi.com/articles/reading-raw-evm-calldata)

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Raise issue](https://github.com/duneanalytics/dune-docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/call-tables)

[Event Logs](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mantle/decoded/event-logs)

⌘I

# linea.traces - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/linea/raw/traces#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Raw

linea.traces

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Analytics Studio](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Catalyst](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `linea.traces` table contains the traces of the transactions executed on the Ethereum Virtual Machine (EVM). It includes the traces of the transaction and the traces of the internal transactions. Traces are the result of the execution of the transaction and are used to debug and understand the execution of the transaction. They are also known as \`internal transactions\` and can be used to understand the execution of a transaction.

This is the raw version of this table. If the chain is a Fully Managed chain, decoded transaction calls will be available, see [call tables](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/linea/decoded/call-tables)
 section. If this is a Hosted chain, decoded call tables will not be available.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Example
-------

### Querying traces for a specific transaction hash

    SELECT *
    FROM linea.traces
    WHERE tx_hash = 0xb30d6d67cf7d148c2257bf598c5f5cdf5912a3d05c7d3b000398d675d2fa912c

YesNo

# Event Logs - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/linea/decoded/event-logs#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=fbdf0e7e6fabc31e49afcdb53cb5e774)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu/logo/dune-logo-dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=uyJ-jHeSRFvNrzyu&q=85&s=767370d661596e21a7b3a4525d50d77e)](https://dune.com/)

Event Logs

[Get Started](https://docs.dune.com/home)
